class="umCUbe"><table class="JC"><tr><td class="GC">Phone</td><td class="tel"><div class="UAa">info@auto-meble.pl</div></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"></td></tr></table></div></div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div class="wz4dC"><div class="r6Rtbe Szu0Jd fNFtPe hRCQgb" role="article"><div class="MLtShf"><div class="vdgRCc"><div class="ZMDitf">Story</div></div></div><div class="A4Urud"><div class="Kem0xf f7g5be"><div class="D0cs5d UVvO7"><div class="cHz88d">Tagline</div><div class="umCUbe">Custom built inside expedition vehicles 4x4 off road - interior design - Zabudowy samochodów terenowych 4x4, wyprawowych off road</div></div><div class="D0cs5d tNqBj"><div class="cHz88d">Introduction</div><div class="umCUbe"><p>
We make interiors for expeditionary off-road 4x4 vehicles. We offer you 
comprehensive service adapting vehicles to the tourist trips outside the
 city or long trips around the world. You can set up your interior to be
 comfortable and functional. We offer you our advice and assistance. Our
 systems of boxes and drawers have several types of finish, all 
affordable. We use wide range of accessories (hinges and locks) with 
heightened wear resistance. Interiors are made of waterproof plywood, 
which is one of the lightest in the world. To compare - 1 m² of our 
plywood weighs as much as 1 m²  aluminum sheet with a thickness of 2 mm.
 Our products are finished with aluminum which additionally protects 
them from destruction and work perfectly in difficult off-road 
conditions.
</p>
<p>
Comprehensive service it’s not only furniture but also places to sleep, 
sink, shower, stove, water tanks with hot water, toilet, compressor, 
side tent with shower, rear tent, roofing and any other accessories you 
like. We install intelligent systems of current control in batteries, 
230V converters and extra batteries. If you use our service you can be 
self-sufficient in every trip because we provide comfort and 
functionality. It doesn’t matter if you want to go for a summer trip out
 of the city or big trip to Africa, you have your own camper. There is 
no need to visit many workshops, because we do everything what is 
necessary to start your trip.
<span style="font-weight:bold">Your comfort during expedition is our success!!!</span>
